name:C‚Äçh‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçf‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äç‚Ñ¢
info:Superior 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Business travelers
info:146 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 6, 2023
msg:Crowne Plaza Tianjin Binhai Shengguang Suites: Crew Paradise

„ÄêJourney Memory„Äë
"The reason why it is called Binhai Shengguang Crowne Plaza is because it is close to Binhai International Airport, not because it is in Binhai New Area. In terms of administrative division, this hotel is in the Airport Economic Zone under the jurisdiction of Dongli District. Don't make a mistake when booking. ‚Äù
There are many intercontinental stores in the Airport Economic Zone. The left and right sides of this CP are Airport Smart Selection and Airport East Zone Smart Selection. There is a wide range of options to choose from. This hotel has been open for 14 years, and I have stayed at it frequently. Generally speaking, the software and hardware have remained at a fairly high level, and there is no sign of any decline.

„ÄêMember Benefits„Äë
"There is a welcome drink coupon."
No administrative trea**ent. No 90 yuan meal coupon. The executive lounge is on the highest floor, and there is also an exclusive lounge for crews on the lower floors. It is close to the airport and there are many crews staying there. It also gives captains, stewardesses and other guests more privacy.

„ÄêGuest Room Snapshot„Äë
"Every time, they upgrade me to an audio-visual suite. There is a projector in the living room, a normal TV in the bedroom, and a small TV in the bathroom. The round bathtub is very unique, and the original storage of the projector has many channels from Shanxi Province. It is speculated that this equipment was purchased from Shanxi, or that the Chinese owner of this hotel is a businessman from Shanxi. Of course, this is just speculation. ‚Äù
Currently, there are 119 CPs in China, including 116 in the Mainland, 1 in Taiwan Province and two in Hong Kong. Although this Holy Light Crown store opened relatively early, its software and services are among the best and worth recommending. Before National Day, the hotels in the Airport Economic Zone here were very ambitious and raised the prices very high. As a result, the passenger flow was shocking. The main guests were still concentrated in the urban area. The occupancy rate of hotels in the suburbs was not high, so in the future Market research and judgment still need to be strengthened.

„ÄêBrief description of public area„Äë
"There is a tennis center on the fourth floor."
The gym and swimming pool are both on the first floor. Although they are not 24 hours a day, in order to take care of red-eye flights, early flights, crew members, business travelers, etc., they are opened at 6 a.m. (the same is true for breakfast, which is considered to be relatively early among the intercontinental hotels in Tianjin). ), the swimming pool and gym will be open, so it‚Äôs better than the best. There is a pool table.

„ÄêCatering Overview„Äë
"There is a dedicated private long table area for breakfast, which is similar to a semi-open box. It is suitable for family guests, high-end VIPs, high-level IHG members, etc."
The pancakes are expertly fried to a crisp. There are many foreign guests, and the density is especially high during the first half of breakfast. It seems that foreigners have the habit of getting up early.

„ÄêFix omissions and omissions„Äë
"All the staff in the hotel are attentive and considerate, especially the duty manager Fu Jing (Nell), who helped me arrange every detail. Tianjin people are like this, kind-hearted, humorous, hospitable, and treat everyone with care. It‚Äôs familiar. For example, I lost my backpack on the luggage rack of the high-speed train, and the conductor Liu Lulu and team member Xiao Wen immediately found it for me, which made me feel warm and cozy. For example, every time I host a scene at the Tianjin Auto Show, I always meet people who run into the luggage rack. Fans, prospective car owners, car owners, and even peers and staff in various exhibition areas come backstage to praise me or express gratitude to me. Sometimes they are even recognized in the subway and receive a flood of compliments. I really like it. Tianjin has such a warm a**osphere."
Tianjin's rail transit is very mature. For example, if you want to go to Binhai Shengguang from Heping Express in the city, you only need to take one stop from Anshan Road Metro Station to Yingkou Road to transfer, and then take three stops to get to Tianjin Station. Transfer to Airport Economic Zone Station and take 8 stops (the journey takes 39 minutes). Take a taxi from Exit B of Airport Economic Zone Station to Binhai Shengguang, which only takes about 10 minutes. There is a large private garden in the atrium on the first floor, suitable for walking.
